.. _ref-api-functions:

**************
|VL| Functions
**************




.. _ref-api-functions-findcircle:

Find Circle ``FindCircle()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	FindCircle
	*	-	Text
		-	Find Circle
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				circleX,circleY,circleRad,iErr,szMsg= imgProcTLS.FindCircle (0,0,xxxScale*656,xxxScale*494,2,50,0,xxxScale*247,0,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds circle contours in the image. Output is the working image with edges and the found circle. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      Col,Row,Radius,iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.FindCircle(
        Col,
        Row,
        Width,
        Hight,
        NumPyramidLevels,
        Edge Threshold,
        Min Radius,
        Max Radius,
        Sub Pixel,
        modeDrawOverlay
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-findcircle:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) and corresponding Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          2:means that search will start from a 2 times subsampled image; original image size: 656x494 pixels; 2times subsampled:164x124 Pixels
        
        
          minimum edge strength that will be considered
        
        
          lower limit for found circles
        
        
          upper limit for found circles
        
        
          1: subpixel accuracy for found circles is activated
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays
        
      

dRectRoiCtr
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	internal_name
		-	dRectRoiCtr
	*	-	allowed
		-	all
	*	-	default
		-	0
	*	-	dialogtype
		-	no_dialog
	*	-	min
		-	all
	*	-	max
		-	all
	*	-	password
		-	
	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text
		-	Rect Roi
	*	-	typ
		-	:ref:`dRECT_CTR <ref-api-structs-drect_ctr>`
	*	-	visible
		-	

.. hint::

	Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) and corresponding Width and Height
          

	

	
          
Row (X):
	Row:   Position X-Value in mm
Col (Y):
	Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
Height:
	Hight: Size in mm
Width:
	Width: Size in mm

iNumPyramidLevels
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	internal_name
		-	iNumPyramidLevels
	*	-	allowed
		-	1,2,3
	*	-	default
		-	0
	*	-	dialogtype
		-	no_dialog
	*	-	min
		-	all
	*	-	max
		-	all
	*	-	password
		-	
	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text
		-	Subsampling
	*	-	typ
		-	:ref:`INT32 <ref-api-structs-int32>`
	*	-	visible
		-	

.. hint::

.. _ref-api-functions-measurefocus:

Measure Focus ``MeasureFocus()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	calibration
	*	-	Name
		-	MeasureFocus
	*	-	Text
		-	Measure Focus
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				dFocusVal,iErr,szMsg= imgProcTLS.MeasureFocus (0,0,xxxScale*656,xxxScale*494,1,0,0)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function determines a focus value. This value has a maximum when the same object is in focus. Different objects have different values. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      dFocusVal,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.MeasureFocus(
        Col,
        Row,
        Width,
        Hight,
        iStep,
        iFocusOperator,
        iSmoothing
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-measurefocus:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) and corresponding Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
                
        
          Which neighbor will be taken:
	1: left and right neighbor
	5: 5 pixels to the left and 5 pixels to the right
        
        
          Operator to be chosen:
	0: modified Laplace
	1: 3x3 Sobel
        
        
          Reduce Image Noise:
	0: none/off
	1: medium 
	2: High

.. _ref-api-functions-findedgecircle2:

Find EdgeCircle ``FindEdgeCircle2()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	FindEdgeCircle2
	*	-	Text
		-	Find EdgeCircle
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				circleX,circley,circleRad,iErr,szMsg= imgProcTLS.FindEdgeCircle (2,0,0,0,xxxScale*80,xxxScale*120,16,xxxScale*20,5,0,0.5,xxxScale*2.0,0,2)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds a circle with the circle approximation of number of searchrays with a given center point. Output is the working image with found edge, region and histogram of edges along search direction.  (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      Col,Row,Radius,iDetectedPoints,iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.FindEdgeCircle(
        Polarity,
        Criteria,
        Col,
        Row,
        Min Radius,
        Max Radius,
        nSearchRays,
        dRectangleWidth,
        Threshold,
        Angle Tolerance,
        Smoothing,
        dDistanceErrorThreshold,
        iHistogramDisplay,
        Overlay
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-findedgecircle2:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Polarity of the edge along search direction
	0: black/white
	1: white/black
	2: both
        
        
          Edge criteria
	0: strongest
	1: first
	2: last
        
        
          circle center point: column/horizontal X and row/vertical Y coordinate; must be inside a possible circle
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          
                
        
          lower limit for found circles
        
        
          upper limit for found circles
        
        
          Number of Searchrays; Minimum: 4 Maximum depends on radius
        
        
          Width of search ray
        
        
          minimum edge strength that will be considered
        
        
          tolerance of edge found [0;+/-10]
        
        
          smoothes edge histogram along search direction [0..3]
        
        
          gauge for circle approximation; if found edge is above distance of possible found circle center point, edge will not be considered
        
        
          displays Histogramm for Searchrays in the overlay Image. OverlayMode must be activated
	0: no Histogramm
	1..Number Searchray: corresponding histogramm
	> Number Searchray: all Histograms will be drawn in the overlay image
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays

.. _ref-api-functions-findsegmentedgecircle2:

Find Segment EdgeCircle ``FindSegmentEdgeCircle2()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	FindSegmentEdgeCircle2
	*	-	Text
		-	Find Segment EdgeCircle
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				circleX,circley,circleRad,iArrayLength,dXArray,dYArray,iErr,szMsg= imgProcTLS.FindSegmentEdgeCircle (2,0,0,0,xxxScale*80,xxxScale*120,16,xxxScale*20,5,0,0.5,xxxScale*2.0,0,2)

	*	-	Level
		-	100
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds a circle with the circle approximation of number of searchrays with a given center point. Output is the working image with found edge, region and histogram of edges along search direction. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)

.. _ref-api-input-findsegmentedgecircle2:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Polarity of the edge along search direction
	0: black/white
	1: white/black
	2: both
        
        
          Edge criteria
	0: strongest
	1: first
	2: last
        
        
          circle center point: column/horizontal X and row/vertical Y coordinate; must be inside a possible circle
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          
                
        
          lower limit for found circles
        
        
          upper limit for found circles
        
        
          Number of Searchrays; Minimum: 4 Maximum depends on radius
        
        
          Width of search ray
        
        
          minimum edge strength that will be considered
        
        
          tolerance of edge found [0;+/-10]
        
        
          smoothes edge histogram along search direction [0..3]
        
        
          gauge for circle approximation; if found edge is above distance of possible found circle center point, edge will not be considered
        
        
          displays Histogramm for Searchrays in the overlay Image. OverlayMode must be activated
	0: no Histogramm
	1..Number Searchray: corresponding histogramm
	> Number Searchray: all Histograms will be drawn in the overlay image
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays

.. _ref-api-functions-findline2:

Find Line ``FindLine2()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	FindLine2
	*	-	Text
		-	Find Line
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				l1LineStartX,l1LineStartY,l1LineEndX,l1LineEndY,l1EdgeStrength,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.FindLine(2,0,0,0,0,xxxScale*50,xxxScale*100,10,10,0.5,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds a line contours in a given region in the image. Output is the working image with found edge, region and histogram of edges along search direction. Parameter 12 is optional. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      L1P1Col,L1P1Row,L1P2Col,L1P2Row,QualityL1,iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.FindLine(
        Polarity,
        Criteria,
        Col,
        Row,
        Angle,
        Width,
        Hight,
        Threshold,
        Angle Tolerance,
        Smoothing,
        [iCamNum],
        Overlay,
        [Image]
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-findline2:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Polarity of the edge along search direction
	0: black/white
	1: white/black
	2: both
        
        
          Edge criteria
	0: strongest
	1: first
	2: last
        
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) of the rotated (angle) rectangle with Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Angle: Angle in Degree
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          minimum edge strength that will be considered
        
        
          tolerance of edge found [0;+/-10]
        
        
          smoothes edge histogram along search direction [0..3]
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays
        
        
          Number of Camera. [Optional Value]
        
        
          Optional Parameter. Default 1.defines Input Image
	0: unchanged camera image
	1: modified working image

          Col Point2:   Position Y-Value of Point2 in mm

          
        
        
          Strength of line
        
        
           0 if operation succeeded

          1 if operation failed
        
        
           no text if operation succeeded

          error text if operation failed

.. _ref-api-functions-findlineincircle:

Find Line in Circle ``FindLineInCircle()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	FindLineInCircle
	*	-	Text
		-	Find Line in Circle
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				l1LineStartX,l1LineStartY,l1LineEndX,l1LineEndY,l1Angle,l1EdgeStrength,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.FindLineInCircle(2,0,0,0,xxxScale*40,xxxScale*160,10,10,0.5,2)

	*	-	Level
		-	100
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds a line contours in around a circle. Output is the working image with found edge, region and histogram of edges along search direction. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)

.. _ref-api-input-findlineincircle:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Polarity of the edge along search direction
	0: black/white
	1: white/black
	2: both
        
        
          Edge criteria
	0: strongest
	1: first
	2: last
        
        
          circle center point: column/horizontal X and row/vertical Y coordinate; must be inside a possible circle
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          
        
        
          lower limit for found circles
        
        
          upper limit for found circles
        
        
          minimum edge strength that will be considered
        
        
          tolerance of edge found [0;+/-10]
        
        
          smoothes edge histogram along search direction [0..3]
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays
        
      

iModePolarity
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

	:widths: 20 80

	*	-	dialogtype
		-	no_dialog
	*	-	min
		-	all
	*	-	max
		-	all
	*	-	password
		-	
	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text

.. _ref-api-functions-findsegment:

Find Segment ``FindSegment()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	FindSegment
	*	-	Text
		-	Find Segment
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				l1LineStartX,l1LineStartY,l1LineEndX,l1LineEndY,l2LineStartX,l2LineStartY,l2LineEndX,l2LineEndY,l1EdgeStrength,l2EdgeStrength,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.FindSegment(2,0,0,0,0,xxxScale*50,xxxScale*100,10,10,0.5,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds a segment in a given region in the image. Output is the working image with found edges, region and histogram of edges along search direction. Parameter 11,12,14,15 is optional. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      L1P1Col,L1P1Row,L1P2Col,L1P2Row,  L2P1Col,L2P1Row,L2P2Col,L2P2Row,  QualityL1,QualityL2,iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.FindSegment(
        Polarity,
        Criteria,
        Col,
        Row,
        Angle,
        Width,
        Hight,
        Threshold,
        Angle Tolerance,
        Smoothing,
        [TargetWidth],
        [TargetWidthTolerance],
        Overlay,
        [Image],
        [iCamNum]
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-findsegment:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Colour of the segment along search direction
	0: white
	1: black
	2: any
        
        
          Segment criteria
	0: strongest
	1: widest
	2: Narrowest
	3: Widest Contigous
        
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) of the rotated (angle) rectangle with Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Angle: Angle in Degree
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          minimum edge strength that will be considered
        
        
          tolerance of edge found [0;+/-10]
        
        
          smoothes edge histogram along search direction [0..3]
        
        
          Target distance between the two lines. Segment with closest result will be used
        
        
          Maximum distance +- between the segment lines referenced to the Target Width 
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays
        
        
          Optional Parameter. Default 1.defines Input Image
	0: unchanged camera image
	1: modified working image
        
        
          Number of Camera. [Optional Value]

.. _ref-api-output-findsegment:

Output Parameters
-----------------

::

	
        
          1st segment line; starting Linepoint: column/horizontal X + row/vertical Y coordinate and ending Linepoint: column + row coordinate
          


          Row Point1:   Position X-Value of Point1 in mm

          Col Point1:   Position Y-Value of Point1 in mm

          Row Point2:   Position X-Value of Point2 in mm

          Col Point2:   Position Y-Value of Point2 in mm

          
        
        
          2nd segment line; starting Linepoint: column/horizontal X + row/vertical Y coordinate and ending Linepoint: column + row coordinate
          


          Row Point1:   Position X-Value of Point1 in mm

          Col Point1:   Position Y-Value of Point1 in mm

          Row Point2:   Position X-Value of Point2 in mm

          Col Point2:   Position Y-Value of Point2 in mm

          
        
        
          Strength of first line
        
        
          Strength of second line
        
        
           0 if operation succeeded

          1 if operation failed
        
        
           no text if operation succeeded

          error text if operation failed

.. _ref-api-functions-binfilter:

binary filter ``BinFilter()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	filter
	*	-	Name
		-	BinFilter
	*	-	Text
		-	binary filter
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.BinFilter(iFilter,dKernelSize)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function applies a morphological operation on a binarized image (values 0:black to 255:white). Output is the working image with two possible value per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for the blob operator. (29.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.BinFilter(
        iFilter,
        iKernelSize
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-binfilter:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Type of morphological filter:
	
          0: erosion
	
          1: dilation
	
          2: Opening
	
          3: Closing
        
        
          iKernelSize in Pixel
	0: 3x3
	1: 5x5
	2: 7x7

.. _ref-api-functions-grayfilter:

Gray filter ``GrayFilter()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	filter
	*	-	Name
		-	GrayFilter
	*	-	Text
		-	Gray filter
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.GrayFilter(iFilter,iKernelSizeV,iKernelSizeH,imgMode,[tiCamNum])

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function applies a morphological operation on a gray image (all values between 0:black and 255:white). Output is the working image with all possible gray values per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for binarization. (29.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.GrayFilter(
        iFilter,
        iKernelSizeV,
        iKernelSizeH,
        imgMode,
        [tiCamNum]
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-grayfilter:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Type of morphological filter:
	
          0: median
	
          1: Gauss
	
          2: erosion
	
          3: dilation
	
          4: Opening
	
          5: Closing
	
          6: HighPass
	
          7: Sharpen
	
          8: Histogramm Streching
        
        
          iKernelSizeH in Pixel
	0: 3x3
	1: 5x5
	...;
	10: 21x21;
        
        
          iKernelSizeH in Pixel
	0: 3x3
	1: 5x5
	...;
	10: 21x21;
        
        
          &nbsp;0: camera image
	1: working image
        
        
          ?

          0: median

	
          1: Gauss

	
          2: erosion

	
          3: dilation

	
          4: Opening

	
          5: Closing

          7: Sharpen

	
          8: Histogramm Streching

.. _ref-api-functions-autocontrast:

AutoContrast ``AutoContrast()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	filter
	*	-	Name
		-	AutoContrast
	*	-	Text
		-	AutoContrast
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.AutoContrast(dPercentageLower,dPercentageUpper,imgMode,[tiCamNum])

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This filter applies a brightness equalization. Bright areas will moved to white and dark areas to black. Output is the working image with all possible gray values per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for binarization. (29.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.AutoContrast(
        dPercentageLower,
        dPercentageUpper,
        imgMode,
        [tiCamNum]
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-autocontrast:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Determines lower Percentage of darkest pixels inside an image will be of gray value 0 (=black)
	0.1: very small fraction of dark pixels will be moved to black color
	25:very big fraction of dark pixels will be moved to black color ;
        
        
          Determines upper Percentage of brighest pixels inside an image will be of gray value 255 (=white)
	0.1: very small fraction of bright pixels will be moved to white color
	25:very big fraction of bright pixels will be moved to white color ;
        
        
          &nbsp;0: camera image
	1: working image
        
        
          ?

.. _ref-api-functions-illuminationcorrection:

IlluminationCorrection ``IlluminationCorrection()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	filter
	*	-	Name
		-	IlluminationCorrection
	*	-	Text
		-	IlluminationCorrection
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.IlluminationCorrection(dClipLimit,iKernelSizeV,iKernelSizeH,imgMode)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Adaptive histogram equalization is used (CLAHE). The image is divided into small blocks called "tiles" (tileSize is 8x8 by default). Then each of these blocks are histogram equalized as usual. Output is the working image with all possible gray values per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for binarization. (29.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.IlluminationCorrection(
        dClipLimit,
        iKernelSizeV,
        iKernelSizeH,
        imgMode
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-illuminationcorrection:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Limits the amplification by clipping the histogram at a predefined value before computing the histogram.
        
        
          Vertical Tile Size  in Pixel
	8: nx8
	10: nx10;
        
        
          Horizontal Tile Size  in Pixel
	8: 8xn
	10: 10xn;
        
        
          &nbsp;0: camera image
	1: working image

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text
		-	Clip Limit
	*	-	typ
		-	:ref:`double <ref-api-structs-double>`
	*	-	visible
		-

	Limits the amplification by clipping the histogram at a predefined value before computing the histogram.

.. _ref-api-functions-sharpengauss:

SharpenGauss ``SharpenGauss()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	filter
	*	-	Name
		-	SharpenGauss
	*	-	Text
		-	SharpenGauss
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.SharpenGauss(dAlpha,dSigma,[Col],[Row],[Width],[Hightt],[iCamNum])

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Gauss smoothed image will be subtracted from the original image. The resulting image will be added with the weighing factor alpha to the original image. Output is the working image with all possible gray values per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for binarization.(29.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.SharpenGauss(
        dAlpha,
        dSigma,
        [Col],
        [Row],
        [Width],
        [Hightt],
        [iCamNum]
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-sharpengauss:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Limits the amplification by clipping the histogram at a predefined value before computing the histogram.
        
        
          Extent of the filter. 
        
         
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) and corresponding Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm [Optional Value]
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm [Optional Value]
	
          Hight: Size in mm [Optional Value]
	
          Width: Size in mm [Optional Value]
	
          
        
        
          &nbsp;0: camera image
	1: working image

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

		-	20
	*	-	max
		-	400
	*	-	password
		-	
	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text
		-	Alpha
	*	-	typ
		-	:ref:`double <ref-api-structs-double>`
	*	-	visible

.. hint::

	Limits the amplification by clipping the histogram at a predefined value before computing the histogram.

.. _ref-api-functions-threshold:

binarization ``Threshold()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	Threshold
	*	-	Text
		-	binarization
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iCalcThreshold,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.Threshold(1,1,128,0)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function binarize the gray value image (values 0:black to 255:white). Output is the working image with two possible value per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for the blob operator. (28.09.2021 TLS563RE)

      dcalcThresh,iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.Threshold(
        ibBright,
        iThreshMode,
        dThresholdLow,
        Image
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-threshold:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Foreground Mode:
	0: Black is foreground
	1: White is foreground
        
        
          automatic Binarization limit
	0: OFF; fixed Limit
	1: automatic
        
        
          Threshold limit for iThresholdMode=0
        
        
          defines Input Image
	0: unchanged camera image
	1: modified working image

.. _ref-api-functions-threshold:

adaptive binarization ``Threshold()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	Threshold
	*	-	Text
		-	adaptive binarization
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.AdaptiveThreshold(0,1,7,3,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function binarize the gray value image (values 0:black to 255:white) locally with automatic Threshold. Output is the working image with two possible value per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for the blob operator. (28.09.2021 TLS563RE)

      iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.AdaptiveThreshold(
        iMethod,
        ibBright,
        iBlocksize,
        dConstantSubMeanVal,
        iBlurBlocksize,
        Image
        )
        

.. _ref-api-input-threshold:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Binarization Mode:
	0: Mean_C
	1: Gaussian_C
        
        
          Foreground Mode:
	0: Black is foreground
	1: White is foreground
        
        
          neighborhood/local environment
	1: 2*1+1=3x3
	2: 2*2+1=5x5
        
        
          Constant subtracted from the mean or weighted mean Default 3; -15..15
        
        
          neighborhood/local environment
	0: none; blurring switched off
	1: 2*1+1=3x3
	2: 2*2+1=5x5
        
        
          defines Input Image
	0: unchanged camera image
	1: modified working image

		-	0

		-	no_dialog

		-	all
	*	-	max
		-	all
	*	-	password
		-	
	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text

	*	-	typ

		-

.. _ref-api-functions-meandevgrayvalue:

MeanDevGrayValue ``MeanDevGrayValue()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	misc
	*	-	Name
		-	MeanDevGrayValue
	*	-	Text
		-	MeanDevGrayValue
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				dMean,dDeviation,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.MeanDevGrayValue(Col,Row,Angle,Width,Hightt,iImg)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function calculates mean gray value and its deviation. Output is the working image with two possible value per pixel 0:background 255:foreground. This image can be used as a base for the blob operator. (29.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      dMean,dDeviation,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.MeanDevGrayValue(
        Col,
        Row,
        Angle,
        Width,
        Hightt,
        iImg
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-meandevgrayvalue:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) of the rotated (angle) rectangle with Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Angle: Angle in Degree
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          defines Input Image
	0: unchanged camera image
	1: modified working image

.. _ref-api-functions-blob:

Blob ``Blob()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	Blob
	*	-	Text
		-	Blob
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iNumBlob,dArea,dCenterC,dCenterR,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.Blob(0,0,xxxScale*656,xxxScale*494,1,0,0,0,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds connected white regions in a binarized image. The image must be binarized with a Threshold opeator. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iNumBlob,Area,Col,Row,Angle,iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.Blob(
        Col,
        Row,
        Width,
        Hight,
        ModeBlob,
        MinSize,
        MaxSize,
        deleteBorderBlobs,
        Overlay
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-blob:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) and corresponding Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
                
        
          searches for smallest/biggest Area:
	0: biggest Area
	1: smallest Area
        
        
          Specifies the minimum number of pixels the region must contain. The default value nMinimumPointsPerRegion = 0 means that no lower bound is checked.
        
        
          Specifies the maximum number of pixels the region may contain. The default value nMaximumPointsPerRegion = 0 means that no upper bound is checked.
        
        
          1: Areas that borders to the edge of a image will not be considered
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays

.. _ref-api-functions-blob2:

Blob2 ``Blob2()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	algorithm functions
	*	-	Name
		-	Blob2
	*	-	Text
		-	Blob2
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				dcalcThresh,iNumBlob,dArea,dCenterC,dCenterR,dAngle,dRectC,dRectR,dRectA,dRectW,dRectH,iErr,szM=imgProcTLS.Blob2(0,0,xxxScale*656,xxxScale*494,1,0,0,0,0,1,1,2,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds connected white regions in a binarized image in a rotated input region. The input image must be a grey value image. Binarization is done in this operator. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iNumBlob,Col,Row,Angle,ScaleCol,ScaleRow,Area,iErr,szMsg = imgProcTLS.Blob2(
        Col,
        Row,
        Angle,
        Width,
        Hight,
        BlobColor,
        ThreshMode,
        ThresholdLow,
        MinSize,
        MaxSize,
        deleteBorderBlobs,
        Unite,
        Overlay,
        Image
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-blob2:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
      
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) of the rotated (angle) rectangle with Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Angle: Angle in Degree
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          Foreground Mode:
	0: Black is foreground
	1: White is foreground
        
        
          automatic Binarization limit
	0: OFF; fixed Limit
	1: automatic
        
        
          Threshold limit for iThresholdMode=0
        
        
          Specifies the minimum number of pixels the region must contain. The default value nMinimumPointsPerRegion = 0 means that no lower bound is checked.
        
        
          Specifies the maximum number of pixels the region may contain. The default value nMaximumPointsPerRegion = 0 means that no upper bound is checked.
        
        
          1: Areas that borders to the edge of a image will not be considered
        
        
          Unites foreground areas.
	0: OFF; biggest area is chosen
	1: unites all areas within Min .. Max Area
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays
        
        
          defines Input Image
	0: unchanged camera image
	1: modified working image

.. _ref-api-output-blob2:

Output Parameters
-----------------

::

	
        
          for iThresholdMode=1 automatically calculated; for iThresholdMode=0: input dThresholdLow
        
        
          number of all found blobs
        
        
          area of biggest/smallest blob
        
        
          blob center point: column/horizontal X and row/vertical Y coordinate
            

            Row:   Position X-Value in mm

            Col:   Position Y-Value in mm

            Angle: Angle in Degree

          
        
        
          angle of blob (principal axis transformation
        
        
          center Point (column and row) of the rotated (angle) rectangle with Width and Height of the resulting bounding box
        
        
           0 if operation succeeded

          1 if operation failed
        
        
           no text if operation succeeded

          error text if operation failed

.. _ref-api-functions-calibrate:

Calibrate ``Calibrate()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	calibration
	*	-	Name
		-	Calibrate
	*	-	Text
		-	Calibrate
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iNumBlob,dCenterC,dCenterR,dAngle,dScaleC,dScaleR,dArea,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.Calibrate(xxxScale*2,xxxScale*1.5,xxxScale*50,0,1,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	This function finds 9 connected white regions in a binarized image. Calibration factors will be derived with the center of each blob. The image must be binarized with a Threshold opeator. An extra big blob can be used to determine positive coordinate axis. (28.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iNumBlob,dCenterC,dCenterR,dAngle,dScaleC,dScaleR,dArea,iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.Calibrate(
        Col,
        Row,
        Width,
        Hight,
        dDistC,
        dDistR,
        iMinSize,
        iMaxSize,
        bdeleteBorderBlobs,
        bBiggestDotForOrientation
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-calibrate:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) and corresponding Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          horizontal distance between blobs in mm
        
        
          vertical distance between blobs in mm
        
        
          Specifies the minimum number of pixels the region must contain. The default value nMinimumPointsPerRegion = 0 means that no lower bound is checked.
        
        
          Specifies the maximum number of pixels the region may contain. The default value nMaximumPointsPerRegion = 0 means that no upper bound is checked.
        
        
          1: Areas that borders to the edge of a image will not be considered
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays

	*	-	visible

.. hint::

Row (X):

Col (Y):
	Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
Height:

Width:

	*	-	max
		-	all
	*	-	password
		-	
	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text
		-	minimum Size
	*	-	typ
		-	:ref:`double <ref-api-structs-double>`
	*	-	visible
		-	

.. hint::

	Specifies the minimum number of pixels the region must contain. The default value nMinimumPointsPerRegion = 0 means that no lower bound is checked.

          adds integer to filename

	This function saves a bitmap image. (30.09.2021 TLS563RE)

        "C:/tmp/image.BMP",
        imgMode,
        [tiCamNum]
        )

	5: stitched image

        Text,
        Col,
        Row,
        Color,
        Scaling,
        Line with,
        Camera Number
        )

----------------

          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm

          1: green
	
           2: red
	
           3: blau
	
           4: pink
	
           5: cyan
	
           6: yellow
	
           7: light red
	
           8: purple

Draw Circle ``DrawCircle()``

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Draws a given circle with radius into an overlay at position Point pt and a chosen color. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.DrawCircle(
        Col,
        Row,
        Radius,
        Color,
        iThicknessPix,
        bRadInPixel,
        bCenterInPixel
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-drawcircle:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          starting Linepoint: column/horizontal X + row/vertical Y coordinate and ending Linepoint: column + row coordinate
          
	
	
          Row Point1:   Position X-Value of Point1 in mm
	
          Col Point1:   Position Y-Value of Point1 in mm
	
          Row Point2:   Position X-Value of Point2 in mm
	
          Col Point2:   Position Y-Value of Point2 in mm
	
          
            
        
          4: color of the graphic 0..254
	
          1: green
	
           2: red
	
           3: blau
	
           4: pink
	
           5: cyan
	
           6: yellow
	
           7: light red
	
           8: purple
	
        
        
          thickness of circle line in pixel
        
        
          1 if coordinates in Pixel or 0 scaled Coordinates in mm

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

.. _ref-api-functions-drawcross:

Draw Cross ``DrawCross()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	graphics
	*	-	Name
		-	DrawCross
	*	-	Text
		-	Draw Cross
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.DrawCross(0,0,xxxScale*100,xxxScale*100,0,2,0)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Draws a given line with start and end point into an overlay with a chosen color. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)

      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.DrawCross(
        Col,
        Row,
        Size,
        Color,
        iThicknessPix,
        bCoordinatesInPixel,
        Camera Number
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-drawcross:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Poit to draw the Cross
	1: column/horizontal X coordinate
	2: row/vertical Y coordinate
        
        
          3: Size of cross line in pixel or mm
        
        
          4: color of the graphic 0..254
	
          1: green
	
           2: red
	
           3: blau
	
           4: pink
	
           5: cyan
	
           6: yellow
	
           7: light red
	
           8: purple
	
        
        
          5: 1 if size in Pixel or 0 scaled size in mm
        
        
          6: 1 if center in Pixel or 0 scaled size in mm

.. _ref-api-functions-drawrectangle:

Draw Rectangle ``DrawRectangle()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	graphics
	*	-	Name
		-	DrawRectangle
	*	-	Text
		-	Draw Rectangle
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.DrawRectangle(0,0,0,xxxScale*200,xxxScale*100,0,2,0,0)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	10th parameter is optional. Default=0.Draws a given rectangle with size (width/height)into an overlay at position Point pt and a chosen color. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)

      iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.Rectangle(
        Col,
        Row,
        Angle,
        Width,
        Hight,
        Color,
        iThicknessPix,
        bSizeInPixel,
        bCenterInPixel,
        bWithOutCal,
        Camera Number
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-drawrectangle:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) of the rotated (angle) rectangle with Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Angle: Angle in Degree
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          4: color of the graphic 0..254
	
          1: green
	
           2: red
	
           3: blau
	
           4: pink
	
           5: cyan
	
           6: yellow
	
           7: light red
	
           8: purple
	
        
        
          thickness of circle line in pixel
        
        
          1 if size in Pixel or 0 scaled size in mm
        
        
          1 if center point in Pixel or 0 scaled center point in mm
        
        
          calibration is not considered.

Draw RectangleID ``DrawRectangleID()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	graphics
	*	-	Name
		-	DrawRectangleID
	*	-	Text
		-	Draw RectangleID
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,szMsg=imgProcTLS.DrawRectangleID(0,0,0,xxxScale*200,xxxScale*100,0,0,1)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Draws a given rectangle with size (width/height)into an overlay at position Point pt with a chosen color and an identification number of the rectangle. (27.09.2021 TLS563RE)
 
      Err,szMsg=imgProcTLS.DrawRectangleID(
          Row,
          Col,
          Angle,
          Hight,
          Width,
          Color,
          size in Pixel,
          Center in Pixel,
          ID,
          Camera Number
          )
      

.. _ref-api-input-drawrectangleid:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Region of Interest: Center Point of RoI (column and row) of the rotated (angle) rectangle with Width and Height
          
	
	
          Row:   Position X-Value in mm
	
          Col:   Position Y-Value in mm
	
          Angle: Angle in Degree
	
          Hight: Size in mm
	
          Width: Size in mm
	
          
        
        
          color of the graphic 0..254
	
          1: green
	
           2: red
	
           3: blau
	
           4: pink
	
           5: cyan
	
           6: yellow
	
           7: light red
	
           8: purple
	
        
        
          1 if label on Corner 
	
          0 label in center
        
        
          1 if center point in Pixel or 0 scaled center point in mm
        
        
          Number of ROI.
        
        
          Number of Camera. [Optional Value]

.. hint::

	this function evaluates thickness of a disc

.. _ref-api-input-getscheibendicke:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          radius horiontally to the left and right / vertically above and below will be found; the center point will be determine independandly; if left and right radius are about the same a right radius will be a result; default value=15Pix
        
        
          tolerance for local minumum; default:10
        
        
          Edge criteria
	0: deactivated
	1: activated
        
        
          start of filename without ".bmp" including pathname
        
        
          defines appearance of output overlay
	0: OFF; no overlay created
	1: take over overlay from former operators 
	2: erases former overlays and displays only Find Line Overlays

		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-

.. _ref-api-functions-setpfomm2hex:

SetPFOmm2Hex ``SetPFOmm2Hex()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	Interface
	*	-	Name
		-	SetPFOmm2Hex
	*	-	Text
		-	SetPFOmm2Hex
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.SetPFOmm2Hex(dScanPosX,dScanPosY,dScanPosZ,dScanPosDefocus)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Prepares PFO coordinates. Transforms coordinates from mm to 10쨉m and HEX Values and build result string. Absolutely necessary before SetPFO2Wait. Must have at least 2 parameter x/y. Can have up to 4 parameters x,y,z,defocus. (30.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.SetPFOmm2Hex(
        dScanPosX,
        dScanPosY,
        dScanPosZ,
        dScanPosDefocus
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-setpfomm2hex:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Scanner Position X. Minimum and Maximum values depends on used optic.
        
        
          Scanner Position Y. Minimum and Maximum values depends on used optic.
        
        
          Scanner Position Z. Minimum and Maximum values depends on used optic. Only considered when PFO-3D used, other neglected.
        
        
          Scanner Position Defocus. Minimum and Maximum values depends on used optic. Only considered when PFO-3D used, other neglected.

.. _ref-api-functions-setpfo2wait:

SetPFO2Wait ``SetPFO2Wait()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	Interface
	*	-	Name
		-	SetPFO2Wait
	*	-	Text
		-	SetPFO2Wait
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				assert(imgProcTLS.SetPFO2Wait(),"Error Waiting for Thread; Algo Error")

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	To be used only in conjunction with SetPFOmm2Hex. Hex Values will be send to the Laser Control Unit and wait for an answer. Script execution will be interruptes as lng as an answer will be received from laser control unit. Uses of this function is blocked in the GUI. (30.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      bOK=imgProcTLS.SetPFO2Wait()
      

.. _ref-api-input-setpfo2wait:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	


.. _ref-api-output-setpfo2wait:

Output Parameters
-----------------

::

	
        
          Result
0: Error; Script execution will be stopped and a error will be sent toi the laser control unit
1: successful

		-	no_dialog

		-	0
	*	-	max
		-	1
	*	-	password
		-	
	*	-	readonly
		-	
	*	-	text
		-	Result
	*	-	typ
		-	:ref:`INT32 <ref-api-structs-int32>`
	*	-	visible
		-	

.. hint::

	Result

	0: Error; Script execution will be stopped and a error will be sent toi the laser control unit

	1: successful



.. _ref-api-functions-output:

Output ``Output()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	Interface
	*	-	Name
		-	Output
	*	-	Text
		-	Output
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.Output(iFirstIndex,dValue,dScaleFactor,dValue,dScaleFactor,...)

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	OldVersion:Prepares Result coordinates; values which will be send to XVARS to the laser control unit. 1st value determine number of values beginning at XVAR1. Must be executed at the end of the sript. Otherwise an error will be send. More than 10 values does not make any sense because of limit space for string . iE,internResultString=imgProcTLS.Output(0) if no variable should be transfered. Resets the whole buffer. (30.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.Output(
        iFirstIndex,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        .
        .
        .
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-output:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Start Number of XVARS. XVAR offset.
        
        
          Result Variable 1.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 2.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 3.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 4.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 5.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 6. 
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 7.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 8.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 9.
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.
        
        
          Result Variable 10. 
        
        
          Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.

	*	-	max
		-	all

		-

		-	
	*	-	text
		-	Scale3 for XVAR
	*	-	typ
		-	:ref:`double <ref-api-structs-double>`
	*	-	visible
		-	

.. hint::

	Scaling factor for Result Variable. Variable in mm. x/y translations sould be scaled for 100um. Angles should be in steps: Angle in degrees *65536/360. All other values should be scaled to 1. Scaling set to 0 means: no consideration of this variable.

.. _ref-api-functions-outputn1:

OutputN1 ``OutputN1()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	Interface
	*	-	Name
		-	OutputN1
	*	-	Text
		-	OutputN1
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.OutputN1(iFirstIndex,dValue,dScaleFactor,gResNameTable["X"],1,65536/360,gResNameTable["Alpha"])

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Writes to 1st Buffer.Resets Buffer. Prepares Result coordinates; values which will be send to XVARS to the laser control unit. 1st value determines start XVAR (x minimum 1 XVAR1). Must be executed at the end of the sript. Otherwise an error will be send. More than 10 values does not make any sense because of limit space for string. (30.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.OutputN1(
        iFirstIndex,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable,
        .
        .
        .
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable
        )
      

.. _ref-api-input-outputn1:

Input Parameters
----------------

::

	
        
          Start Number of XVARS. XVAR offset.
        
        
          Result Variable 1. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 2. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 3. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 4. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 5. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 6. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 7. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 8.

.. _ref-api-functions-outputntemp1:

OutputNTemp1 ``OutputNTemp1()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	Interface
	*	-	Name
		-	OutputNTemp1
	*	-	Text
		-	OutputNTemp1
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.OutputNTemp1(iFirstIndex,dValue,dScaleFactor,gResNameTable["X"],1,65536/360,gResNameTable["Alpha"])

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Writes to 1st Buffer. Buffer is not reset!! Prepares Result coordinates; values which will be send to XVARS to the laser control unit. 1st value determines start XVAR (x minimum 1 XVAR1). Must be executed at the end of the sript. Otherwise an error will be send. More than 10 values does not make any sense because of limit space for string.  (30.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.OutputNTemp1(
        iFirstIndex,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable,
        .
        .
        .
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable
        )

	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 2. 
	Value: in mm. 
	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 
	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 
	Scaling: 1 in other case

.. _ref-api-functions-outputntemp1:

OutputNTemp1 ``OutputNTemp1()``
=====================================================================

.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col
.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80
	:header-rows: 0
	:stub-columns: 1

	*	-	Class.. rst-class:: right-align-left-col

		-	Interface
	*	-	Name
		-	OutputNTemp1
	*	-	Text
		-	OutputNTemp1
	*	-	ExecutionText
		-	.. code-block:: lua

				iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.OutputNTemp1(iFirstIndex,dValue,dScaleFactor,gResNameTable["X"],1,65536/360,gResNameTable["Alpha"])

	*	-	Level
		-	
	*	-	Icon
		-	

.. hint::

	Writes to 2nd Buffer. Buffer is not reset!! Prepares Result coordinates; values which will be send to XVARS to the laser control unit. 1st value determines start XVAR (x minimum 1 XVAR1). Must be executed at the end of the sript. Otherwise an error will be send. More than 10 values does not make any sense because of limit space for string. (30.09.2021 TLS563RE)
      
      iErr,internResultString=imgProcTLS.OutputNTemp1(
        iFirstIndex,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable,
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable,
        .
        .
        .
        dValue,
        dScaleFactor,
        gResNameTable
        )

	Scaling: 1 in other case 
	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.
        
        
          Result Variable 2.

	Value: in mm. 

	Scaling: 100 in case of x/y translation. 

	Scaling: 65536/360 in case of angles 

	Scaling: 1 in other case 

	Meaning of variable for plausibilty checks in MulitScripting.

.. hint::

	Sleep time in ms.


.. _ref-api-output-sleep:

Output Parameters
-----------------

::

	
        
          Differntial Time since last Start of Time
        
        
           0 if operation succeeded

          1 if operation failed
        
        
           no text if operation succeeded

          error text if operation failed
